    38	type PagesFromDataTemplateContext interface {
    39	        // AddPage adds a new page to the site.
    40	        // The first return value will always be an empty string.
    41	        AddPage(any) (string, error)
    42	
    43	        // AddResource adds a new resource to the site.
    44	        // The first return value will always be an empty string.
    45	        AddResource(any) (string, error)
    46	
    47	        // The site to which the pages will be added.
    48	        Site() page.Site
    49	
    50	        // The same template may be executed multiple times for multiple languages.
    51	        // The Store can be used to store state between these invocations.
    52	        Store() *hstore.Scratch
    53	
    54	        // By default, the template will be executed for the language
    55	        // defined by the _content.gotmpl file (e.g. its mount definition).
    56	        // This method can be used to activate the template for all languages.
    57	        // The return value will always be an empty string.
    58	        EnableAllLanguages() string
    59	}
    60	
    61	var _ PagesFromDataTemplateContext = (*pagesFromDataTemplateContext)(nil)
    62	
    63	type pagesFromDataTemplateContext struct {
    64	        p *PagesFromTemplate
    65	}
    66	
    67	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) toPathSitesMap(v any) (string, map[string]any, map[string]any, error) {
    68	        m, err := hmaps.ToStringMapE(v)
    69	        if err != nil {
    70	                return "", nil, nil, err
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        path, err := cast.ToStringE(m["path"])
    74	        if err != nil {
    75	                return "", nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid path %q", path)
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        sites := hmaps.ToStringMap(m["sites"])
    79	
    80	        return path, sites, m, nil
    81	}
    82	
    83	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) AddPage(v any) (string, error) {
    84	        path, sites, m, err := p.toPathSitesMap(v)
    85	        if err != nil {
    86	                return "", err
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        hash, hasChanged := p.p.buildState.checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(path, sites, m)
    90	        if !hasChanged {
    91	                return "", nil
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        pe := &pagemeta.PageConfigEarly{
    95	                IsFromContentAdapter: true,
    96	                Frontmatter:          m,
    97	                SourceEntryHash:      hash,
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        // The rest will be handled after the cascade is calculated and applied.
   101	        if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(pe.Frontmatter, pe); err != nil {
   102	                err = fmt.Errorf("failed to decode page map: %w", err)
   103	                return "", err
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        if err := pe.Init(true); err != nil {
   107	                return "", err
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        p.p.buildState.NumPagesAdded++
   111	
   112	        return "", p.p.HandlePage(p.p, pe)
   113	}
   114	
   115	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) AddResource(v any) (string, error) {
   116	        path, sites, m, err := p.toPathSitesMap(v)
   117	        if err != nil {
   118	                return "", err
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        hash, hasChanged := p.p.buildState.checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(path, sites, m)
   122	        if !hasChanged {
   123	                return "", nil
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        var rd pagemeta.ResourceConfig
   127	        if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(m, &rd); err != nil {
   128	                return "", err
   129	        }
   130	        rd.ContentAdapterSourceEntryHash = hash
   131	
   132	        p.p.buildState.NumResourcesAdded++
   133	
   134	        if err := rd.Validate(); err != nil {
   135	                return "", err
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return "", p.p.HandleResource(p.p, &rd)
   139	}
   140	
   141	func (p *pagesFromDataTemplateContext) Site() page.Site {
   142	        return p.p.Site
   143	}

   146	        return p.p.store
   147	}

   150	        p.p.buildState.EnableAllLanguages = true
   151	        return ""
   152	}

   156	        return ""

   159	func NewPagesFromTemplate(opts PagesFromTemplateOptions) *PagesFromTemplate {
   160	        return &PagesFromTemplate{
   161	                PagesFromTemplateOptions: opts,
   162	                PagesFromTemplateDeps:    opts.DepsFromSite(opts.Site),
   163	                buildState: &BuildState{
   164	                        sourceInfosCurrent: hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo](),
   165	                },
   166	                store: hstore.NewScratch(),
   167	        }
   168	}

   180

   182	}

   190	type PagesFromTemplate struct {
   191	        PagesFromTemplateOptions
   192	        PagesFromTemplateDeps
   193	        buildState *BuildState
   194	        store      *hstore.Scratch
   195	}
   196	
   197	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) AddChange(id identity.Identity) {
   198	        b.buildState.ChangedIdentities = append(b.buildState.ChangedIdentities, id)
   199	}
   200	
   201	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) MarkStale() {
   202	        b.buildState.StaleVersion++
   203	}

   205	func (b *PagesFromTemplate) StaleVersion() uint32 {

   208	
   209	type BuildInfo struct {
   210	        NumPagesAdded       uint64
   211	        NumResourcesAdded   uint64
   212	        EnableAllLanguages  bool
   213	        EnableAllDimensions bool
   214	        ChangedIdentities   []identity.Identity
   215	        DeletedPaths        []PathHashes
   216	        Path                *paths.Path
   217	}
   218	
   219	type BuildState struct {
   220	        StaleVersion uint32
   221	
   222	        EnableAllLanguages  bool
   223	        EnableAllDimensions bool
   224	
   225	        // PathHashes deleted in the current build.
   226	        DeletedPaths []PathHashes
   227	
   228	        // Changed identities in the current build.
   229	        ChangedIdentities []identity.Identity
   230	
   231	        NumPagesAdded     uint64
   232	        NumResourcesAdded uint64
   233	
   234	        sourceInfosCurrent  *hmaps.Cache[string, *sourceInfo]
   235	        sourceInfosPrevious *hmaps.Cache[string, *sourceInfo]
   236	}
   237	
   238	func (b *BuildState) hash(v any) uint64 {
   239	        return hashing.HashUint64(v)
   240	}
   241	
   242	type sourceInfo struct {
   243	        siteHashes map[uint64]uint64
   244	}
   245	
   246	func (b *BuildState) checkHasChangedAndSetSourceInfo(changedPath string, sites map[string]any, v any) (uint64, bool) {
   247	        hv := b.hash(v)
   248	        hsites := b.hash(sites)
   249	
   250	        si, _ := b.sourceInfosCurrent.GetOrCreate(changedPath, func() (*sourceInfo, error) {
   251	                return &sourceInfo{
   252	                        siteHashes: make(map[uint64]uint64),
   253	                }, nil
   254	        })
   255	
   256	        if h, found := si.siteHashes[hsites]; found && h == hv {
   257	                return hv, false
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        if psi, found := b.sourceInfosPrevious.Get(changedPath); found {
   261	                if h, found := psi.siteHashes[hsites]; found && h == hv {
   262	                        // Not changed.
   263	                        si.siteHashes[hsites] = hv
   264	                        return hv, false
   265	                }
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        // It has changed.
   269	        si.siteHashes[hsites] = hv
   270	        return hv, true
   271	}
   272	
   273	type PathHashes struct {
   274	        Path   string
   275	        Hashes map[uint64]struct{}
   276	}
   277	
   278	func (b *BuildState) resolveDeletedPaths() {
   279	        if b.sourceInfosPrevious == nil {
   280	                b.DeletedPaths = nil
   281	                return
   282	        }
   283	        var pathsHashes []PathHashes
   284	        b.sourceInfosPrevious.ForEeach(func(k string, pv *sourceInfo) bool {
   285	                if cv, found := b.sourceInfosCurrent.Get(k); !found {
   286	                        pathsHashes = append(pathsHashes, PathHashes{Path: k, Hashes: map[uint64]struct{}{}})
   287	                } else {
   288	                        deleted := map[uint64]struct{}{}
   289	                        for k, ph := range pv.siteHashes {
   290	                                ch, found := cv.siteHashes[k]
   291	                                if !found || ch != ph {
   292	                                        deleted[ph] = struct{}{}
   293	                                }
   294	                        }
   295	                        if len(deleted) > 0 {
   296	                                pathsHashes = append(pathsHashes, PathHashes{Path: k, Hashes: deleted})
   297	                        }
   298	                }
   299	                return true
   300	        })
   301	
   302	        b.DeletedPaths = pathsHashes
   303	}
   304	
   305	func (b *BuildState) PrepareNextBuild() {
   306	        b.sourceInfosPrevious = b.sourceInfosCurrent
   307	        b.sourceInfosCurrent = hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo]()
   308	        b.StaleVersion = 0
   309	        b.DeletedPaths = nil
   310	        b.ChangedIdentities = nil
   311	        b.NumPagesAdded = 0
   312	        b.NumResourcesAdded = 0
   313	}
   314	
   315	func (p PagesFromTemplate) CloneForSite(s page.Site) *PagesFromTemplate {
   316	        // We deliberately make them share the same DependencyManager and Store.
   317	        p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.Site = s
   318	        p.PagesFromTemplateDeps = p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.DepsFromSite(s)
   319	        p.buildState = &BuildState{
   320	                sourceInfosCurrent: hmaps.NewCache[string, *sourceInfo](),
   321	        }
   322	        return &p
   323	}
   324	
   325	func (p PagesFromTemplate) CloneForGoTmpl(fi hugofs.FileMetaInfo) *PagesFromTemplate {
   326	        p.PagesFromTemplateOptions.GoTmplFi = fi
   327	        return &p
   328	}
   329	
   330	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) GetDependencyManagerForScope(scope int) identity.Manager {
   331	        return p.DependencyManager
   332	}
   333	
   334	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) GetDependencyManagerForScopesAll() []identity.Manager {
   335	        return []identity.Manager{p.DependencyManager}
   336	}
   337	
   338	func (p *PagesFromTemplate) Execute(ctx context.Context) (BuildInfo, error) {
   339	        defer func() {
   340	                p.buildState.PrepareNextBuild()
   341	        }()
   342	
   343	        f, err := p.GoTmplFi.Meta().Open()
   344	        if err != nil {
   345	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   346	        }
   347	        defer f.Close()
   348	
   349	        tmpl, err := p.TemplateStore.TextParse(filepath.ToSlash(p.GoTmplFi.Meta().Filename), helpers.ReaderToString(f))
   350	        if err != nil {
   351	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   352	        }
   353	
   354	        data := &pagesFromDataTemplateContext{
   355	                p: p,
   356	        }
   357	
   358	        ctx = tpl.Context.DependencyManagerScopedProvider.Set(ctx, p)
   359	
   360	        if err := p.TemplateStore.ExecuteWithContext(ctx, tmpl, io.Discard, data); err != nil {
   361	                return BuildInfo{}, err
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        if p.Watching {
   365	                p.buildState.resolveDeletedPaths()
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        bi := BuildInfo{
   369	                NumPagesAdded:       p.buildState.NumPagesAdded,
   370	                NumResourcesAdded:   p.buildState.NumResourcesAdded,
   371	                EnableAllLanguages:  p.buildState.EnableAllLanguages,
   372	                EnableAllDimensions: p.buildState.EnableAllDimensions,
   373	                ChangedIdentities:   p.buildState.ChangedIdentities,
   374	                DeletedPaths:        p.buildState.DeletedPaths,
   375	                Path:                p.GoTmplFi.Meta().PathInfo,
   376	        }
   377	
   378	        return bi, nil
   379	}

    45	type DatesStrings struct {
    46	        Date        string `json:"date"`
    47	        Lastmod     string `json:"lastMod"`
    48	        PublishDate string `json:"publishDate"`
    49	        ExpiryDate  string `json:"expiryDate"`
    50	}
    51	
    52	type Dates struct {
    53	        Date        time.Time
    54	        Lastmod     time.Time
    55	        PublishDate time.Time
    56	        ExpiryDate  time.Time
    57	}
    58	
    59	func (d Dates) String() string {
    60	        fmtDate := func(t time.Time) string {
    61	                if t.IsZero() {
    62	                        return "<zero>"
    63	                }
    64	                return t.Format(time.RFC3339)
    65	        }
    66	        return fmt.Sprintf("Date: %s, Lastmod: %s, PublishDate: %s, ExpiryDate: %s",
    67	                fmtDate(d.Date), fmtDate(d.Lastmod), fmtDate(d.PublishDate), fmtDate(d.ExpiryDate))
    68	}
    69	
    70	func (d Dates) IsDateOrLastModAfter(in Dates) bool {
    71	        return d.Date.After(in.Date) || d.Lastmod.After(in.Lastmod)
    72	}
    73	
    74	func (d *Dates) UpdateDateAndLastmodAndPublishDateIfAfter(in Dates) {
    75	        if in.Date.After(d.Date) {
    76	                d.Date = in.Date
    77	        }
    78	        if in.Lastmod.After(d.Lastmod) {
    79	                d.Lastmod = in.Lastmod
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        if in.PublishDate.After(d.PublishDate) && in.PublishDate.Before(htime.Now()) {
    83	                d.PublishDate = in.PublishDate
    84	        }
    85	}
    86	
    87	func (d Dates) IsAllDatesZero() bool {
    88	        return d.Date.IsZero() && d.Lastmod.IsZero() && d.PublishDate.IsZero() && d.ExpiryDate.IsZero()
    89	}
    90	
    91	const (
    92	        pageMetaKeySites  = "sites"
    93	        pageMetaKeyMarkup = "markup"
    94	)
    95	
    96	func (pcfg *PageConfigEarly) SetMetaPreFromMap(ext string, frontmatter map[string]any, logger loggers.Logger, conf config.AllProvider) error {
    97	        if frontmatter != nil {
    98	                if err := pcfg.setFromFrontMatter(frontmatter); err != nil {
    99	                        return err
   100	                }
   101	        }
   102	        return pcfg.resolveContentType(ext, conf.GetConfigSection("mediaTypes").(media.Types))
   103	}
   104	
   105	func (pcfg *PageConfigEarly) setFromFrontMatter(frontmatter map[string]any) error {
   106	        // Needed for case insensitive fetching of params values.
   107	        hmaps.PrepareParams(frontmatter)
   108	        pcfg.Frontmatter = frontmatter
   109	
   110	        if v, found := frontmatter[pageMetaKeyMarkup]; found {
   111	                pcfg.Content.Markup = cast.ToString(v)
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        if v, found := frontmatter[pageMetaKeySites]; found {
   115	                if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(v, &pcfg.Sites); err != nil {
   116	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to decode sites from front matter: %w", err)
   117	                }
   118	        }
   119	        return nil
   120	}
   121	
   122	func (p *PageConfigEarly) setCascadeEarlyValueIfNotSet(key string, value any) (done bool) {
   123	        switch key {
   124	        case pageMetaKeySites:
   125	                p.Sites.SetFromParamsIfNotSet(value.(hmaps.Params))
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        return !p.Sites.Matrix.IsZero()
   129	}

   148	// PageConfig configures a Page, typically from front matter.

   152	        Dates Dates `json:"-"` // Dates holds the four core dates for this page.
   153	        DatesStrings
   154	        Params hmaps.Params // User defined params.
   155	
   156	        Title          string   // The title of the page.
   157	        LinkTitle      string   // The link title of the page.
   158	        Type           string   // The content type of the page.
   159	        Layout         string   // The layout to use for to render this page.
   160	        Weight         int      // The weight of the page, used in sorting if set to a non-zero value.
   161	        URL            string   // The URL to the rendered page, e.g. /sect/mypage.html.
   162	        Slug           string   // The slug for this page.
   163	        Description    string   // The description for this page.
   164	        Summary        string   // The summary for this page.
   165	        Draft          bool     // Whether or not the content is a draft.
   166	        Headless       bool     `json:"-"` // Whether or not the page should be rendered.
   167	        IsCJKLanguage  bool     // Whether or not the content is in a CJK language.
   168	        TranslationKey string   // The translation key for this page.
   169	        Keywords       []string // The keywords for this page.
   170	        Aliases        []string // The aliases for this page.
   171	        Outputs        []string // The output formats to render this page in. If not set, the site's configured output formats for this page kind will be used.
   172	
   173	        FrontMatterOnlyValues `mapstructure:"-" json:"-"`
   174	
   175	        Sitemap config.SitemapConfig
   176	        Build   BuildConfig
   177	        Menus   any // Can be a string, []string or map[string]any.
   178

   180	        ContentAdapterData map[string]any `mapstructure:"-" json:"-"`
   181	
   182	        // Compiled values.
   183	        ConfiguredOutputFormats output.Formats `mapstructure:"-" json:"-"`
   184	}

   186	// SitesMatrixAndComplements holds a sites matrix and a sites complements configuration.
   187	type SitesMatrixAndComplements struct {
   188	        SitesMatrix      sitesmatrix.VectorStore `mapstructure:"-" json:"-"`
   189	        SitesComplements sitesmatrix.VectorStore `mapstructure:"-" json:"-"`
   190	}
   191	
   192	// MatchSiteVector checks whether the site vector matches the sites matrix.
   193	func (p *SitesMatrixAndComplements) MatchSiteVector(siteVector sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   194	        return p.SitesMatrix.HasAnyVector(siteVector)
   195	}
   196	
   197	// MatchLanguageCoarse checks whether the language dimension matches either
   198	// the sites matrix or the sites complements.
   199	func (p *SitesMatrixAndComplements) MatchLanguageCoarse(siteVector sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   200	        i := siteVector.Language()
   201	        return p.SitesMatrix.HasLanguage(i) || p.SitesComplements.HasLanguage(i)
   202	}
   203	
   204	// MatchRoleCoarse checks whether the role dimension matches either
   205	// the sites matrix or the sites complements.
   206	func (p *SitesMatrixAndComplements) MatchRoleCoarse(siteVector sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   207	        i := siteVector.Role()
   208	        return p.SitesMatrix.HasRole(i) || p.SitesComplements.HasRole(i)
   209	}
   210	
   211	// MatchVersionCoarse checks whether the version dimension matches either
   212	// the sites matrix or the sites complements.
   213	func (p *SitesMatrixAndComplements) MatchVersionCoarse(siteVector sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   214	        i := siteVector.Version()
   215	        return p.SitesMatrix.HasVersion(i) || p.SitesComplements.HasVersion(i)
   216	}

   218	func DefaultPageConfig() *PageConfigLate {
   219	        return &PageConfigLate{
   220	                Build: DefaultBuildConfig,
   221	        }
   222	}
   223	
   224	func (p *PageConfigEarly) Init(pagesFromData bool) error {
   225	        if pagesFromData {
   226	                p.Path = strings.TrimPrefix(p.Path, "/")
   227	
   228	                if p.Path == "" && p.Kind != kinds.KindHome {
   229	                        return fmt.Errorf("empty path is reserved for the home page")
   230	                }
   231	
   232	                if p.Content.Markup != "" {
   233	                        return errors.New("markup must not be set, use mediaType")
   234	                }
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        return nil
   238	}
   239	
   240	func (p *PageConfigLate) Init() error {
   241	        return nil
   242	}
   243	
   244	func buildSitesComplementsFromSitesConfig(
   245	        conf config.AllProvider,
   246	        fim *hugofs.FileMeta,
   247	        sitesConfig sitesmatrix.Sites,
   248	) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
   249	        if sitesConfig.Complements.IsZero() {
   250	                if fim != nil && fim.SitesComplements != nil {
   251	                        return fim.SitesComplements
   252	                }
   253	                return sitesmatrix.NilStore
   254	        }
   255	        intsetsCfg := sitesmatrix.IntSetsConfig{
   256	                Globs: sitesConfig.Complements,
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        sitesComplements := sitesmatrix.NewIntSetsBuilder(conf.ConfiguredDimensions()).WithConfig(intsetsCfg)
   260	
   261	        if fim != nil && fim.SitesComplements != nil {
   262	                sitesComplements.WithDimensionsFromOtherIfNotSet(fim.SitesComplements)
   263	        }
   264	
   265	        return sitesComplements.Build()
   266	}
   267	
   268	func buildSitesMatrixFromSitesConfig(
   269	        conf config.AllProvider,
   270	        sitesMatrixBase sitesmatrix.VectorIterator,
   271	        sitesConfig sitesmatrix.Sites,
   272	) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
   273	        if sitesConfig.Matrix.IsZero() && sitesMatrixBase != nil {
   274	                if sitesMatrixBase.LenVectors() == 1 {
   275	                        return conf.ConfiguredDimensions().GetOrCreateSingleVectorStore(sitesMatrixBase.VectorSample())
   276	                }
   277	                return sitesmatrix.VectorIteratorToStore(sitesMatrixBase)
   278	        }
   279	
   280	        if conf.ConfiguredDimensions().IsSingleVector() {
   281	                return conf.ConfiguredDimensions().CommonSitesMatrix.DefaultSite
   282	        }
   283	
   284	        intsetsCfg := sitesmatrix.IntSetsConfig{
   285	                Globs: sitesConfig.Matrix,
   286	        }
   287	        sitesMatrixPage := sitesmatrix.NewIntSetsBuilder(conf.ConfiguredDimensions()).WithConfig(intsetsCfg)
   288	
   289	        if sitesMatrixBase != nil {
   290	                sitesMatrixPage.WithDimensionsFromOtherIfNotSet(sitesMatrixBase)
   291	        }
   292	        sitesMatrixPage.WithDefaultsIfNotSet()
   293	
   294	        matrix := sitesMatrixPage.Build()
   295	
   296	        return matrix
   297	}
   298	
   299	func (p *PageConfigEarly) CompileEarly(pi *paths.Path, cascades *page.PageMatcherParamsConfigs,
   300	        conf config.AllProvider, fim *hugofs.FileMeta, sitesMatrixBase sitesmatrix.VectorIterator, sitesMatrixBaseOnly bool,
   301	) error {
   302	        // First apply the cascades with no site filtering.
   303	        for cascade := range cascades.All() {
   304	                if cascade.Target.SitesMatrixCompiled != nil {
   305	                        continue
   306	                }
   307	
   308	                if !cascade.Target.Match(p.Kind, pi.Base(), conf.Environment(), p.SitesMatrix) {
   309	                        continue
   310	                }
   311	
   312	                for ck, cv := range cascade.Fields {
   313	                        if done := p.setCascadeEarlyValueIfNotSet(ck, cv); done {
   314	                                break
   315	                        }
   316	                }
   317	
   318	        }
   319	
   320	        if sitesMatrixBaseOnly {
   321	                p.SitesMatrix = sitesmatrix.VectorIteratorToStore(sitesMatrixBase)
   322	        } else {
   323	                p.SitesMatrix = buildSitesMatrixFromSitesConfig(
   324	                        conf,
   325	                        sitesMatrixBase,
   326	                        p.Sites,
   327	                )
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        // Finally apply the cascades with site filtering.
   331	        // These may also contain site specific settings,
   332	        // so preserve the original matrix for comparison.
   333	        sitesMatrixBefore := p.Sites.Matrix
   334	        var hadCascadeMatch bool
   335	
   336	        for cascade := range cascades.All() {
   337	                if cascade.Target.SitesMatrixCompiled == nil {
   338	                        continue
   339	                }
   340	
   341	                if !cascade.Target.Match(p.Kind, pi.Base(), conf.Environment(), p.SitesMatrix) {
   342	                        continue
   343	                }
   344	
   345	                hadCascadeMatch = true
   346	
   347	                for ck, cv := range cascade.Fields {
   348	                        if done := p.setCascadeEarlyValueIfNotSet(ck, cv); done {
   349	                                break
   350	                        }
   351	                }
   352	
   353	        }
   354	
   355	        if hadCascadeMatch && !sitesMatrixBaseOnly && !sitesMatrixBefore.Equal(p.Sites.Matrix) {
   356	                // Matrix has changed, rebuild.
   357	                p.SitesMatrix = buildSitesMatrixFromSitesConfig(
   358	                        conf,
   359	                        sitesMatrixBase,
   360	                        p.Sites,
   361	                )
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        p.SitesComplements = buildSitesComplementsFromSitesConfig(
   365	                conf,
   366	                fim,
   367	                p.Sites,
   368	        )
   369	
   370	        mediaTypes := conf.GetConfigSection("mediaTypes").(media.Types)
   371	        if err := p.resolveContentType(pi.Ext(), mediaTypes); err != nil {
   372	                return err
   373	        }
   374	
   375	        return nil
   376	}
   377	
   378	func (p *PageConfigEarly) CompileForPagesFromDataPre(basePath string, logger loggers.Logger, mediaTypes media.Types) error {
   379	        // In content adapters, we always get relative paths.
   380	        if basePath != "" {
   381	                p.Path = path.Join(basePath, p.Path)
   382	        }
   383	
   384	        if p.Kind == "" {
   385	                p.Kind = kinds.KindPage
   386	        }
   387	
   388	        // Note that NormalizePathStringBasic will make sure that we don't preserve the unnormalized path.
   389	        // We do that when we create pages from the file system; mostly for backward compatibility,
   390	        // but also because people tend to use use the filename to name their resources (with spaces and all),
   391	        // and this isn't relevant when creating resources from an API where it's easy to add textual meta data.
   392	        p.Path = paths.NormalizePathStringBasic(p.Path)
   393	
   394	        return p.resolveContentType("", mediaTypes)
   395	}
   396	
   397	func (p *PageConfigEarly) resolveContentType(ext string, mediaTypes media.Types) error {
   398	        if p.Content.Markup == "" && p.Content.MediaType == "" {
   399	                if ext == "" {
   400	                        ext = "md"
   401	                }
   402	                p.ContentMediaType = MarkupToMediaType(ext, mediaTypes)
   403	                if p.ContentMediaType.IsZero() {
   404	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to resolve media type for suffix %q", ext)
   405	                }
   406	        }
   407	
   408	        var s string
   409	        if p.ContentMediaType.IsZero() {
   410	                if p.Content.MediaType != "" {
   411	                        s = p.Content.MediaType
   412	                        p.ContentMediaType, _ = mediaTypes.GetByType(s)
   413	                }
   414	
   415	                if p.ContentMediaType.IsZero() && p.Content.Markup != "" {
   416	                        s = p.Content.Markup
   417	                        p.ContentMediaType = MarkupToMediaType(s, mediaTypes)
   418	                }
   419	        }
   420	
   421	        if p.ContentMediaType.IsZero() {
   422	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to resolve media type for %q", s)
   423	        }
   424	
   425	        if p.Content.Markup == "" {
   426	                p.Content.Markup = p.ContentMediaType.SubType
   427	        }
   428	        return nil
   429	}
   430	
   431	// Compile sets up the page configuration after all fields have been set.
   432	func (p *PageConfigLate) Compile(e *PageConfigEarly, logger loggers.Logger, outputFormats output.Formats) error {
   433	        if e.IsFromContentAdapter {
   434	                if err := mapstructure.WeakDecode(p.ContentAdapterData, p); err != nil {
   435	                        err = fmt.Errorf("failed to decode page map: %w", err)
   436	                        return err
   437	                }
   438	        }
   439	
   440	        if p.Params == nil {
   441	                p.Params = make(hmaps.Params)
   442	        } else {
   443	                hmaps.PrepareParams(p.Params)
   444	        }
   445	
   446	        if len(p.Outputs) > 0 {
   447	                outFormats, err := outputFormats.GetByNames(p.Outputs...)
   448	                if err != nil {
   449	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to resolve output formats %v: %w", p.Outputs, err)
   450	                } else {
   451	                        p.ConfiguredOutputFormats = outFormats
   452	                }
   453	        }
   454	
   455	        return nil
   456	}
   457	
   458	// MarkupToMediaType converts a markup string to a media type.
   459	func MarkupToMediaType(s string, mediaTypes media.Types) media.Type {
   460	        s = strings.ToLower(s)
   461	        mt, _ := mediaTypes.GetBestMatch(markup.ResolveMarkup(s))
   462	        return mt
   463	}

   526	type Source struct {
   527	        // MediaType is the media type of the content.
   528	        MediaType string
   529	
   530	        // The markup used in Value. Only used in front matter.
   531	        Markup string
   532	
   533	        // The content.
   534	        Value any
   535	}
   536	
   537	func (s Source) IsZero() bool {
   538	        return !hreflect.IsTruthful(s.Value)
   539	}
   540	
   541	func (s Source) IsResourceValue() bool {
   542	        _, ok := s.Value.(resource.Resource)
   543	        return ok
   544	}
   545	
   546	func (s Source) ValueAsString() string {
   547	        if s.Value == nil {
   548	                return ""
   549	        }
   550	        ss, err := cast.ToStringE(s.Value)
   551	        if err != nil {
   552	                panic(fmt.Errorf("content source: failed to convert %T to string: %s", s.Value, err))
   553	        }
   554	        return ss
   555	}
   556	
   557	func (s Source) ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser() hugio.OpenReadSeekCloser {
   558	        return hugio.NewOpenReadSeekCloser(hugio.NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(s.ValueAsString()))
   559	}

    96	// cloneWithMetadataFromResourceConfigIfNeeded clones the given resource with the given metadata if the resource supports it.
    97	func cloneWithMetadataFromResourceConfigIfNeeded(rc *pagemeta.ResourceConfig, r resource.Resource) resource.Resource {
    98	        wmp, ok := r.(resource.WithResourceMetaProvider)
    99	        if !ok {
   100	                return r
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        if rc.Name == "" && rc.Title == "" && len(rc.Params) == 0 {
   104	                // No metadata.
   105	                return r
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        if rc.Title == "" {
   109	                rc.Title = rc.Name
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        wrapped := &metaResource{
   113	                name:   rc.Name,
   114	                title:  rc.Title,
   115	                params: rc.Params,
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        return wmp.WithResourceMeta(wrapped)
   119	}
   120	
   121	// CloneWithMetadataFromMapIfNeeded clones the given resource with the given metadata if the resource supports it.
   122	func CloneWithMetadataFromMapIfNeeded(m []map[string]any, r resource.Resource) resource.Resource {
   123	        wmp, ok := r.(resource.WithResourceMetaProvider)
   124	        if !ok {
   125	                return r
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        wrapped := &metaResource{
   129	                name:   r.Name(),
   130	                title:  r.Title(),
   131	                params: r.Params(),
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        assignMetadata(m, wrapped)
   135	        if !wrapped.changed {
   136	                return r
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        return wmp.WithResourceMeta(wrapped)
   140	}
   141	
   142	// AssignMetadata assigns the given metadata to those resources that supports updates
   143	// and matching by wildcard given in `src` using `filepath.Match` with lower cased values.
   144	// This assignment is additive, but the most specific match needs to be first.
   145	// The `name` and `title` metadata field support shell-matched collection it got a match in.
   146	// See https://golang.org/pkg/path/#Match
   147	func assignMetadata(metadata []map[string]any, ma *metaResource) error {
   148	        counters := make(map[string]int)
   149	
   150	        var (
   151	                nameSet, titleSet                   bool
   152	                nameCounter, titleCounter           = 0, 0
   153	                nameCounterFound, titleCounterFound bool
   154	                resourceSrcKey                      = strings.ToLower(ma.Name())
   155	        )
   156	
   157	        for _, meta := range metadata {
   158	                src, found := meta["src"]
   159	                if !found {
   160	                        return fmt.Errorf("missing 'src' in metadata for resource")
   161	                }
   162	
   163	                srcKey := strings.ToLower(cast.ToString(src))
   164	
   165	                glob, err := hglob.GetGlob(srcKey)
   166	                if err != nil {
   167	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to match resource with metadata: %w", err)
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                match := glob.Match(resourceSrcKey)
   171	
   172	                if match {
   173	                        if !nameSet {
   174	                                name, found := meta["name"]
   175	                                if found {
   176	                                        name := cast.ToString(name)
   177	                                        // Bundled resources in sub folders are relative paths with forward slashes. Make sure any renames also matches that format:
   178	                                        name = paths.TrimLeading(filepath.ToSlash(name))
   179	                                        if !nameCounterFound {
   180	                                                nameCounterFound = strings.Contains(name, counterPlaceHolder)
   181	                                        }
   182	                                        if nameCounterFound && nameCounter == 0 {
   183	                                                counterKey := "name_" + srcKey
   184	                                                nameCounter = counters[counterKey] + 1
   185	                                                counters[counterKey] = nameCounter
   186	                                        }
   187	
   188	                                        ma.setName(replaceResourcePlaceholders(name, nameCounter))
   189	                                        nameSet = true
   190	                                }
   191	                        }
   192	
   193	                        if !titleSet {
   194	                                title, found := meta["title"]
   195	                                if found {
   196	                                        title := cast.ToString(title)
   197	                                        if !titleCounterFound {
   198	                                                titleCounterFound = strings.Contains(title, counterPlaceHolder)
   199	                                        }
   200	                                        if titleCounterFound && titleCounter == 0 {
   201	                                                counterKey := "title_" + srcKey
   202	                                                titleCounter = counters[counterKey] + 1
   203	                                                counters[counterKey] = titleCounter
   204	                                        }
   205	                                        ma.setTitle((replaceResourcePlaceholders(title, titleCounter)))
   206	                                        titleSet = true
   207	                                }
   208	                        }
   209	
   210	                        params, found := meta["params"]
   211	                        if found {
   212	                                m := hmaps.ToStringMap(params)
   213	                                // Needed for case insensitive fetching of params values
   214	                                hmaps.PrepareParams(m)
   215	                                ma.updateParams(m)
   216	                        }
   217	                }
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        return nil
   221	}
   222	
   223	func replaceResourcePlaceholders(in string, counter int) string {
   224	        return strings.Replace(in, counterPlaceHolder, strconv.Itoa(counter), -1)
   225	}

    49	func NewSpec(
    50	        s *helpers.PathSpec,
    51	        common *SpecCommon, // may be nil
    52	        wasmDispatchers *warpc.Dispatchers,
    53	        fileCaches filecache.Caches,
    54	        memCache *dynacache.Cache,
    55	        incr identity.Incrementer,
    56	        logger loggers.Logger,
    57	        errorHandler herrors.ErrorSender,
    58	        execHelper *hexec.Exec,
    59	        buildClosers types.CloseAdder,
    60	        rebuilder Rebuilder,
    61	) (*Spec, error) {
    62	        conf := s.Cfg.GetConfig().(*allconfig.Config)
    63	        imgConfig := conf.Imaging
    64	
    65	        imagesDebugl := logger.DebugCommand("images")
    66	        imagesWarnl := logger.WarnCommand("images")
    67	
    68	        imaging, err := images.NewImageProcessor(imagesDebugl, imagesWarnl, wasmDispatchers, imgConfig)
    69	        if err != nil {
    70	                return nil, err
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        if incr == nil {
    74	                incr = &identity.IncrementByOne{}
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        if logger == nil {
    78	                logger = loggers.NewDefault()
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        permalinks, err := page.NewPermalinkExpander(s.URLize, conf.Permalinks)
    82	        if err != nil {
    83	                return nil, err
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        if common == nil {
    87	                common = &SpecCommon{
    88	                        incr:       incr,
    89	                        FileCaches: fileCaches,
    90	                        PostBuildAssets: &PostBuildAssets{
    91	                                PostProcessResources: make(map[string]postpub.PostPublishedResource),
    92	                                JSConfigBuilder:      jsconfig.NewBuilder(),
    93	                        },
    94	                }
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        rs := &Spec{
    98	                PathSpec:     s,
    99	                Logger:       logger,
   100	                ErrorSender:  errorHandler,
   101	                BuildClosers: buildClosers,
   102	                Rebuilder:    rebuilder,
   103	                Imaging:      imaging,
   104	                ImageCache: newImageCache(
   105	                        fileCaches.ImageCache(),
   106	                        memCache,
   107	                        s,
   108	                ),
   109	                ExecHelper: execHelper,
   110	
   111	                Permalinks: permalinks,
   112	
   113	                SpecCommon: common,
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        rs.ResourceCache = newResourceCache(rs, memCache)
   117	
   118	        return rs, nil
   119	}

   163	func (r *Spec) NewResourceWrapperFromResourceConfig(rc *pagemeta.ResourceConfig) (resource.Resource, error) {
   164	        content := rc.Content
   165	        switch r := content.Value.(type) {
   166	        case resource.Resource:
   167	                return cloneWithMetadataFromResourceConfigIfNeeded(rc, r), nil
   168	        default:
   169	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create resource for path %q, expected a resource.Resource, got %T", rc.PathInfo.Path(), content.Value)
   170	        }
   171	}
   172	
   173	// NewResource creates a new Resource from the given ResourceSourceDescriptor.
   174	func (r *Spec) NewResource(rd ResourceSourceDescriptor) (resource.Resource, error) {
   175	        if err := rd.init(r); err != nil {
   176	                return nil, err
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        dir, name := path.Split(rd.TargetPath)
   180	        dir = paths.ToSlashPreserveLeading(dir)
   181	        if dir == "/" {
   182	                dir = ""
   183	        }
   184	        rp := internal.ResourcePaths{
   185	                File:            name,
   186	                Dir:             dir,
   187	                BaseDirTarget:   rd.BasePathTargetPath,
   188	                BaseDirLink:     rd.BasePathRelPermalink,
   189	                TargetBasePaths: rd.TargetBasePaths,
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        isImage := rd.MediaType.MainType == "image"
   193	        var imgFormat images.Format
   194	        var imgOpsSupport images.ImageResourceType
   195	        if isImage {
   196	                imgFormat, imgOpsSupport = images.ImageFormatFromMediaSubType(rd.MediaType.SubType)
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        gr := &genericResource{
   200	                Staler:           &AtomicStaler{},
   201	                h:                &resourceHash{},
   202	                publishInit:      &hsync.OnceMore{},
   203	                keyInit:          &sync.Once{},
   204	                includeHashInKey: isImage,
   205	                paths:            rp,
   206	                spec:             r,
   207	                sd:               rd,
   208	                params:           rd.Params,
   209	                name:             rd.NameOriginal,
   210	                title:            rd.Title,
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        if imgOpsSupport >= images.ImageResourceTypeMetaOnly {
   214	                ir := newImageResource(images.NewImage(imgFormat, r.Imaging, nil, gr), gr)
   215	                return newResourceAdapter(gr.spec, rd.LazyPublish, ir), nil
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        return newResourceAdapter(gr.spec, rd.LazyPublish, gr), nil
   219	}
   220	
   221	func (r *Spec) MediaTypes() media.Types {
   222	        return r.Cfg.GetConfigSection("mediaTypes").(media.Types)
   223	}
   224	
   225	func (r *Spec) OutputFormats() output.Formats {
   226	        return r.Cfg.GetConfigSection("outputFormats").(output.Formats)
   227	}

   230	        return r.Cfg.GetConfigSection("build").(config.BuildConfig)

   234	        return "spec"

   133	func (p *resourceSource) nodeSourceEntryID() any {
   134	        if p.rc != nil {
   135	                return p.rc.ContentAdapterSourceEntryHash
   136	        }
   137	        if p.fi != nil {
   138	                return p.fi.Meta().Filename
   139	        }
   140	        return p.path
   141	}
   142	
   143	func (p *resourceSource) lookupContentNode(v sitesmatrix.Vector) contentNode {
   144	        if p.state >= resourceStateAssigned {
   145	                if p.sv == v {
   146	                        return p
   147	                }
   148	                return nil
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        // A site has not been assigned yet.
   152	
   153	        if p.rc != nil && p.rc.MatchSiteVector(v) {
   154	                return p
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        if p.rc != nil && p.rc.SitesMatrix.LenVectors() > 0 {
   158	                // Do not consider file mount matrix if the resource config has its own.
   159	                return nil
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        if p.fi != nil && p.fi.Meta().SitesMatrix.HasVector(v) {
   163	                return p
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        return nil
   167	}
   168	
   169	func (p *resourceSource) lookupContentNodes(siteVector sitesmatrix.Vector, fallback bool) iter.Seq[contentNodeForSite] {
   170	        if siteVector == p.sv {
   171	                return func(yield func(n contentNodeForSite) bool) {
   172	                        yield(p)
   173	                }
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        pc := p.rc
   177	
   178	        var found bool
   179	        if !fallback {
   180	                if pc != nil && pc.MatchSiteVector(siteVector) {
   181	                        found = true
   182	                } else {
   183	                        return nil
   184	                }
   185	        }
   186	
   187	        if !found && pc != nil {
   188	                if !pc.MatchLanguageCoarse(siteVector) {
   189	                        return nil
   190	                }
   191	                if !pc.MatchVersionCoarse(siteVector) {
   192	                        return nil
   193	                }
   194	                if !pc.MatchRoleCoarse(siteVector) {
   195	                        return nil
   196	                }
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        if !found && !fallback {
   200	                return nil
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        return func(yield func(n contentNodeForSite) bool) {
   204	                if !yield(p) {
   205	                        return
   206	                }
   207	        }
   208	}
   209	
   210	func (r *resourceSource) Path() string {
   211	        return r.path.Base()
   212	}
   213	
   214	func (r *resourceSource) PathInfo() *paths.Path {
   215	        return r.path
   216	}

   562	func (m *pageMap) getResourcesForPage(ps *pageState) (resource.Resources, error) {
   563	        var res resource.Resources
   564	        m.forEachResourceInPage(ps, doctree.LockTypeNone, true, nil, func(resourceKey string, n contentNode) (bool, error) {
   565	                switch n := n.(type) {
   566	                case *resourceSource:
   567	                        r := n.r
   568	                        if r == nil {
   569	                                panic(fmt.Sprintf("getResourcesForPage: resource %q for page %q has no resource, sites matrix %v/%v", resourceKey, ps.Path(), ps.siteVector(), n.sv))
   570	                        }
   571	
   572	                        res = append(res, r)
   573	                case *pageState:
   574	                        res = append(res, n)
   575	                default:
   576	                        panic(fmt.Sprintf("getResourcesForPage: unknown type %T", n))
   577	                }
   578	
   579	                return false, nil
   580	        })
   581	        return res, nil
   582	}

Now I'm getting a clearer picture. Let me look at the `Source.ValueAsString()` method and the `OpenReadSeekCloser` to understand the issue better.

The issue is about `content.value` being set to the string returned by a global resource's `.Content` value. When you call `.Content` on a resource, it returns the content as a string. When you then pass this string as `content.value` to create a new page resource, there's a race condition or caching issue.

Let me look at how `ValueAsString()` and `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()` work:

Looking at line 557-559 of `page_frontmatter.go`:
```go
func (s Source) ValueAsString() string {
    if s.Value == nil {
        return ""
    }
    ss, err := cast.ToStringE(s.Value)
    if err != nil {
        panic(fmt.Errorf("content source: failed to convert %T to string: %s", s.Value, err))
    }
    return ss
}

func (s Source) ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser() hugio.OpenReadSeekCloser {
    return hugio.NewOpenReadSeekCloser(hugio.NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(s.ValueAsString()))
}
```

And in `content_map_page_assembler.go` line 1233:
```go
rd.OpenReadSeekCloser = rc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()
```

So when the content value is a string (like from `.Content`), it creates an `OpenReadSeekCloser` from that string. This should be fine...

But wait, look at line 1194-1204:
```go
if rs.rc != nil && rs.rc.Content.IsResourceValue() {
    if rs.rc.Name == "" {
        rs.rc.Name = relPathOriginal
    }
    r, err := ps.s.ResourceSpec.NewResourceWrapperFromResourceConfig(rs.rc)
    ...
    rs.r = r
    return false, nil
}
```

So if `Content.Value` is a `resource.Resource`, it takes a different path. But if it's a string (from `.Content`), it goes through the normal path at line 1216-1249.

Now let me look at `NewResourceWrapperFromResourceConfig`:

```go
func (r *Spec) NewResourceWrapperFromResourceConfig(rc *pagemeta.ResourceConfig) (resource.Resource, error) {
    content := rc.Content
    switch r := content.Value.(type) {
    case resource.Resource:
        return cloneWithMetadataFromResourceConfigIfNeeded(rc, r), nil
    default:
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create resource for path %q, expected a resource.Resource, got %T", rc.PathInfo.Path(), content.Value)
    }
}
```

So the `IsResourceValue()` check determines which path to take. Let me look more at what `.Content` returns on a resource.

   135	func TestPagesFromGoTmplAsciiDocAndSimilar(t *testing.T) {
   136	        files := `
   137	-- hugo.toml --
   138	disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap"]
   139	baseURL = "https://example.com"
   140	[security]
   141	[security.exec]
   142	allow = ['asciidoctor', 'pandoc','rst2html', 'python']
   143	-- layouts/single.html --
   144	|Content: {{ .Content }}|Title: {{ .Title }}|Path: {{ .Path }}|
   145	-- content/docs/_content.gotmpl --
   146	{{ $.AddPage (dict "path" "asciidoc" "content" (dict "value" "Mark my words, #automation is essential#." "mediaType" "text/asciidoc" )) }}
   147	{{ $.AddPage (dict "path" "pandoc" "content" (dict "value" "This ~~is deleted text.~~" "mediaType" "text/pandoc" )) }}
   148	{{ $.AddPage (dict "path" "rst" "content" (dict "value" "This is *bold*." "mediaType" "text/rst" )) }}
   149	{{ $.AddPage (dict "path" "org" "content" (dict "value" "the ability to use +strikethrough+ is a plus" "mediaType" "text/org" )) }}
   150	{{ $.AddPage (dict "path" "nocontent" "title" "No Content" ) }}
   151	
   152	        `
   153	
   154	        b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
   155	
   156	        if ok, _ := asciidocext.Supports(); ok {
   157	                b.AssertFileContent("public/docs/asciidoc/index.html",
   158	                        "Mark my words, <mark>automation is essential</mark>",
   159	                        "Path: /docs/asciidoc|",
   160	                )
   161	        }
   162	        if pandoc.Supports() {
   163	                b.AssertFileContent("public/docs/pandoc/index.html",
   164	                        "This <del>is deleted text.</del>",
   165	                        "Path: /docs/pandoc|",
   166	                )
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        if rst.Supports() {
   170	                b.AssertFileContent("public/docs/rst/index.html",
   171	                        "This is <em>bold</em>",
   172	                        "Path: /docs/rst|",
   173	                )
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        b.AssertFileContent("public/docs/org/index.html",
   177	                "the ability to use <del>strikethrough</del> is a plus",
   178	                "Path: /docs/org|",
   179	        )
   180	
   181	        b.AssertFileContent("public/docs/nocontent/index.html", "|Content: |Title: No Content|Path: /docs/nocontent|")
   182	}

   184	func TestPagesFromGoTmplAddPageErrors(t *testing.T) {
   185	        filesTemplate := `
   186	-- hugo.toml --
   187	disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap"]
   188	baseURL = "https://example.com"
   189	-- content/docs/_content.gotmpl --
   190	{{ $.AddPage  DICT }}
   191	`
   192	
   193	        t.Run("AddPage, missing Path", func(t *testing.T) {
   194	                files := strings.ReplaceAll(filesTemplate, "DICT", `(dict "kind" "page" "title" "p1")`)
   195	                b, err := hugolib.TestE(t, files)
   196	                b.Assert(err, qt.IsNotNil)
   197	                b.Assert(err.Error(), qt.Contains, "_content.gotmpl:1:4")
   198	                b.Assert(err.Error(), qt.Contains, "error calling AddPage: empty path is reserved for the home page")
   199	        })
   200	
   201	        t.Run("Site methods not ready", func(t *testing.T) {
   202	                filesTemplate := `
   203	-- hugo.toml --
   204	disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap"]
   205	baseURL = "https://example.com"
   206	-- content/docs/_content.gotmpl --
   207	{{ .Site.METHOD }}
   208	`
   209	
   210	                for _, method := range []string{"RegularPages", "Pages", "AllPages", "AllRegularPages", "Home", "Sections", "GetPage", "Menus", "MainSections", "Taxonomies"} {
   211	                        t.Run(method, func(t *testing.T) {
   212	                                files := strings.ReplaceAll(filesTemplate, "METHOD", method)
   213	                                b, err := hugolib.TestE(t, files)
   214	                                b.Assert(err, qt.IsNotNil)
   215	                                b.Assert(err.Error(), qt.Contains, fmt.Sprintf("error calling %s: this method cannot be called before the site is fully initialized", method))
   216	                        })
   217	                }
   218	        })
   219	}

   303	func TestPagesFromGoTmplEditOverlappingContentFile(t *testing.T) {
   304	        t.Parallel()
   305	        files := `
   306	-- hugo.toml --
   307	disableLiveReload = true
   308	disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap"]
   309	-- layouts/all.html --
   310	All: {{ .Content }}|{{ .Title }}|
   311	-- layouts/section.html --
   312	Title: {{ .Title}}|
   313	RegularPages: {{ range .RegularPages }}{{ .Title }}:{{ .Path }}|{{ end }}|
   314	-- content/mysection/_index.md --
   315	---
   316	title: "My Section"
   317	---
   318	-- content/mysection/p1.md --
   319	---
   320	title: "p1 content file"
   321	---
   322	Content of p1
   323	-- content/_content.gotmpl --
   324	{{ $.AddPage (dict "kind" "page" "path" "mysection/p2" "title" "p2 content adapter") }}
   325	`
   326	        b := hugolib.TestRunning(t, files)
   327	        b.AssertFileContent("public/mysection/index.html", "Title: My Section|", "RegularPages: p1 content file:/mysection/p1|p2 content adapter:/mysection/p2|")
   328	
   329	        b.EditFileReplaceAll("content/mysection/p1.md", `"p1 content file"`, `"p1 content file edited"`).Build()
   330	        b.AssertFileContent("public/mysection/index.html", "RegularPages: p1 content file edited:/mysection/p1|p2 content adapter:/mysection/p2|")
   331	
   332	        b.EditFileReplaceAll("content/mysection/_index.md", "My Section", "My Section edited").Build()
   333	        b.AssertFileContent("public/mysection/index.html", "Title: My Section edited|", "RegularPages: p1 content file edited:/mysection/p1|p2 content adapter:/mysection/p2|")
   334	
   335	        b.RemoveFiles("content/mysection/p1.md").Build()
   336	        b.AssertFileContent("public/mysection/index.html", "Title: My Section edited|\nRegularPages: p2 content adapter:/mysection/p2|")
   337	
   338	        b.RemoveFiles("content/_content.gotmpl", "public/mysection/index.html").Build()
   339	        b.AssertFileContent("public/mysection/index.html", "Title: My Section edited|\nRegularPages: |")
   340	}

    62	type ResourceSourceDescriptor struct {
    63	        // The source content.
    64	        OpenReadSeekCloser hugio.OpenReadSeekCloser
    65	
    66	        // The canonical source path.
    67	        Path *paths.Path
    68	
    69	        // The normalized name of the resource.
    70	        NameNormalized string
    71	
    72	        // The name of the resource as it was read from the source.
    73	        NameOriginal string
    74	
    75	        // The title of the resource.
    76	        Title string
    77	
    78	        // Any base paths prepended to the target path. This will also typically be the
    79	        // language code, but setting it here means that it should not have any effect on
    80	        // the permalink.
    81	        // This may be several values. In multihost mode we may publish the same resources to
    82	        // multiple targets.
    83	        TargetBasePaths []string
    84	
    85	        TargetPath           string
    86	        BasePathRelPermalink string
    87	        BasePathTargetPath   string
    88	        SourceFilenameOrPath string // Used for error logging.
    89	
    90	        // The Data to associate with this resource.
    91	        Data map[string]any
    92	
    93	        // The Params to associate with this resource.
    94	        Params hmaps.Params
    95	
    96	        // Delay publishing until either Permalink or RelPermalink is called. Maybe never.
    97	        LazyPublish bool
    98	
    99	        // Set when its known up front, else it's resolved from the target filename.
   100	        MediaType media.Type
   101

   103	        DependencyManager identity.Manager

   106	        // If this is not set, an Identity is created.

   110	func (fd *ResourceSourceDescriptor) init(r *Spec) error {
   111	        if len(fd.TargetBasePaths) == 0 {
   112	                // If not set, we publish the same resource to all hosts.
   113	                fd.TargetBasePaths = r.MultihostTargetBasePaths
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        if fd.OpenReadSeekCloser == nil {
   117	                panic(errors.New("OpenReadSeekCloser is nil"))
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        if fd.TargetPath == "" {
   121	                panic(errors.New("RelPath is empty"))
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        if fd.Params == nil {
   125	                fd.Params = make(hmaps.Params)
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        if fd.Path == nil {
   129	                fd.Path = r.Cfg.PathParser().Parse("", fd.TargetPath)
   130	        }

    32	func newResourceCache(rs *Spec, memCache *dynacache.Cache) *ResourceCache {
    33	        return &ResourceCache{
    34	                fileCache: rs.FileCaches.AssetsCache(),
    35	                cacheResource: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, resource.Resource](
    36	                        memCache,
    37	                        "/res1",
    38	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnChange, Weight: 40},
    39	                ),
    40	                cacheResourceFile: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, resource.Resource](
    41	                        memCache,
    42	                        "/res2",
    43	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnChange, Weight: 40},
    44	                ),
    45	                CacheResourceRemote: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, resource.Resource](
    46	                        memCache,
    47	                        "/resr",
    48	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnChange, Weight: 40},
    49	                ),
    50	                cacheResources: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, resource.Resources](
    51	                        memCache,
    52	                        "/ress",
    53	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnRebuild, Weight: 40},
    54	                ),
    55	                cacheResourceTransformation: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, *resourceAdapterInner](
    56	                        memCache,
    57	                        "/res1/tra",
    58	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnChange, Weight: 40},
    59	                ),
    60	
    61	                cacheResourceTransformationPublished: hmaps.NewMap[string, string](),
    62	        }
    63	}
    64	
    65	type ResourceCache struct {
    66	        sync.RWMutex
    67	
    68	        cacheResource               *dynacache.Partition[string, resource.Resource]
    69	        cacheResourceFile           *dynacache.Partition[string, resource.Resource]
    70	        CacheResourceRemote         *dynacache.Partition[string, resource.Resource]
    71	        cacheResources              *dynacache.Partition[string, resource.Resources]
    72	        cacheResourceTransformation *dynacache.Partition[string, *resourceAdapterInner]
    73	
    74	        // Used in rebuilds. Maps the target path to the last published transformation key.
    75	        cacheResourceTransformationPublished *hmaps.Map[string, string]
    76	
    77	        fileCache *filecache.Cache
    78	}
    79	
    80	func (c *ResourceCache) cleanKey(key string) string {
    81	        return strings.TrimPrefix(path.Clean(strings.ToLower(filepath.ToSlash(key))), "/")
    82	}
    83	
    84	func (c *ResourceCache) Get(ctx context.Context, key string) (resource.Resource, bool) {
    85	        return c.cacheResource.Get(ctx, key)
    86	}
    87	
    88	func (c *ResourceCache) GetOrCreate(key string, f func() (resource.Resource, error)) (resource.Resource, error) {
    89	        return c.cacheResource.GetOrCreate(key, func(key string) (resource.Resource, error) {
    90	                return f()
    91	        })
    92	}

    96	                return f()
    97	        })
    98	}
    99	
   100	func (c *ResourceCache) GetOrCreateResources(key string, f func() (resource.Resources, error)) (resource.Resources, error) {
   101	        return c.cacheResources.GetOrCreate(key, func(key string) (resource.Resources, error) {
   102	                return f()
   103	        })
   104	}
   105	
   106	func (c *ResourceCache) getFilenames(key string) (string, string) {
   107	        filenameMeta := key + ".json"
   108	        filenameContent := key + ".content"
   109	
   110	        return filenameMeta, filenameContent
   111	}
   112	
   113	func (c *ResourceCache) getFromFile(key string) (filecache.ItemInfo, io.ReadCloser, transformedResourceMetadata, bool) {
   114	        c.RLock()
   115	        defer c.RUnlock()
   116	
   117	        var meta transformedResourceMetadata
   118	        filenameMeta, filenameContent := c.getFilenames(key)
   119	
   120	        jsonContent, _ := c.fileCache.GetBytes(filenameMeta)
   121	        if jsonContent == nil {
   122	                return filecache.ItemInfo{}, nil, meta, false
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        if err := json.Unmarshal(jsonContent, &meta); err != nil {
   126	                return filecache.ItemInfo{}, nil, meta, false
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        fi, rc, _ := c.fileCache.Get(filenameContent)
   130	
   131	        return fi, rc, meta, rc != nil
   132	}
   133	
   134	// writeMeta writes the metadata to file and returns a writer for the content part.
   135	func (c *ResourceCache) writeMeta(key string, meta transformedResourceMetadata) (filecache.ItemInfo, io.WriteCloser, error) {
   136	        filenameMeta, filenameContent := c.getFilenames(key)
   137	        raw, err := json.Marshal(meta)
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return filecache.ItemInfo{}, nil, err
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        _, fm, err := c.fileCache.WriteCloser(filenameMeta)
   143	        if err != nil {
   144	                return filecache.ItemInfo{}, nil, err
   145	        }
   146	        defer fm.Close()
   147	
   148	        if _, err := fm.Write(raw); err != nil {
   149	                return filecache.ItemInfo{}, nil, err
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        fi, fc, err := c.fileCache.WriteCloser(filenameContent)
   153	
   154	        return fi, fc, err
   155	}
   156

    28	// ImageCache is a cache for image resources. The backing caches are shared between all sites.
    29	type ImageCache struct {
    30	        pathSpec *helpers.PathSpec
    31	
    32	        fcache *filecache.Cache
    33	        mcache *dynacache.Partition[string, *resourceAdapter]
    34	}
    35	
    36	func (c *ImageCache) getOrCreate(
    37	        parent *imageResource, conf images.ImageConfig,
    38	        createImage func() (*imageResource, image.Image, error),
    39	) (*resourceAdapter, error) {
    40	        relTarget := parent.relTargetPathFromConfig(conf, parent.getSpec().Imaging.Cfg.SourceHash)
    41	        relTargetPath := relTarget.TargetPath()
    42	        memKey := relTargetPath
    43	
    44	        // For multihost sites, we duplicate language versions of the same resource,
    45	        // so we need to include the language in the key.
    46	        // Note that we don't need to include the language in the file cache key,
    47	        // as the hash will take care of any different content.
    48	        if c.pathSpec.Cfg.IsMultihost() {
    49	                memKey = c.pathSpec.Lang() + memKey
    50	        }
    51	        memKey = dynacache.CleanKey(memKey)
    52	
    53	        v, err := c.mcache.GetOrCreate(memKey, func(key string) (*resourceAdapter, error) {
    54	                var img *imageResource
    55	
    56	                // These funcs are protected by a named lock.
    57	                // read clones the parent to its new name and copies
    58	                // the content to the destinations.
    59	                read := func(info filecache.ItemInfo, r io.ReadSeeker) error {
    60	                        img = parent.clone(nil)
    61	                        targetPath := img.getResourcePaths()
    62	                        targetPath.File = relTarget.File
    63	                        img.setTargetPath(targetPath)
    64	                        img.setOpenSource(func() (hugio.ReadSeekCloser, error) {
    65	                                return c.fcache.Fs.Open(info.Name)
    66	                        })
    67	                        img.setSourceFilenameIsHash(true)
    68	                        img.setMediaType(conf.TargetFormat.MediaType())
    69	                        img.Format = conf.TargetFormat
    70	
    71	                        if err := img.InitConfig(r); err != nil {
    72	                                return err
    73	                        }
    74	
    75	                        return nil
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                // create creates the image and encodes it to the cache (w).
    79	                create := func(info filecache.ItemInfo, w io.WriteCloser) (err error) {
    80	                        defer w.Close()
    81	
    82	                        var conv image.Image
    83	                        img, conv, err = createImage()
    84	                        if err != nil {
    85	                                return
    86	                        }
    87	                        targetPath := img.getResourcePaths()
    88	                        targetPath.File = relTarget.File
    89	                        img.setTargetPath(targetPath)
    90	                        img.setOpenSource(func() (hugio.ReadSeekCloser, error) {
    91	                                return c.fcache.Fs.Open(info.Name)
    92	                        })
    93	                        return img.EncodeTo(conf, conv, w)
    94	                }
    95	
    96	                // Now look in the file cache.
    97	
    98	                // The definition of this counter is not that we have processed that amount
    99	                // (e.g. resized etc.), it can be fetched from file cache,
   100	                //  but the count of processed image variations for this site.
   101	                c.pathSpec.ProcessingStats.Incr(&c.pathSpec.ProcessingStats.ProcessedImages)
   102	
   103	                _, err := c.fcache.ReadOrCreate(relTargetPath, read, create)
   104	                if err != nil {
   105	                        return nil, err
   106	                }
   107	
   108	                imgAdapter := newResourceAdapter(parent.getSpec(), true, img)
   109	
   110	                return imgAdapter, nil
   111	        })
   112	
   113	        return v, err
   114	}
   115	
   116	func newImageCache(fileCache *filecache.Cache, memCache *dynacache.Cache, ps *helpers.PathSpec) *ImageCache {
   117	        return &ImageCache{
   118	                fcache: fileCache,
   119	                mcache: dynacache.GetOrCreatePartition[string, *resourceAdapter](
   120	                        memCache,
   121	                        "/imgs",
   122	                        dynacache.OptionsPartition{ClearWhen: dynacache.ClearOnChange, Weight: 70},
   123	                ),
   124	                pathSpec: ps,
   125	        }
   126	}

Now let me think about this more carefully. The error message is:

> error calling Resize: failed to resize image "/home/kijana/Code/hugo-forum-topic-54852/content/products/_content.gotmpl": resize /products/window-frame/01.jpg: invalid JPEG format: short Huffman data

This is about resizing an image. The image is created via content adapter using `content.value` set to the string returned by a global resource's `.Content` value.

1. A global resource (an image) is loaded
2. Its `.Content` (a string) is passed as `content.value` to create a page resource

    25	        io.ReadSeeker

    29	// Sizer provides the size of, typically, a io.Reader.
    30	// As implemented by e.g. os.File and io.SectionReader.
    31	type Sizer interface {
    32	        Size() int64
    33	}

    36	        io.Reader
    37	        Sizer
    38	}

    40	// ToSizeReader converts the given io.Reader to a SizeReader.
    41	// Note that if r is not a SizeReader, the entire content will be read into memory
    42	func ToSizeReader(r io.Reader) (SizeReader, error) {
    43	        if sr, ok := r.(SizeReader); ok {
    44	                return sr, nil
    45	        }
    46	        b, err := io.ReadAll(r)
    47	        if err != nil {
    48	                return nil, err
    49	        }
    50	        return bytes.NewReader(b), nil
    51	}

    53	// CloserFunc is an adapter to allow the use of ordinary functions as io.Closers.

    55	
    56	func (f CloserFunc) Close() error {
    57	        return f()
    58	}

    62	        ReadSeekCloser() (ReadSeekCloser, error)
    63	}
    64	
    65	// readSeekerNopCloser implements ReadSeekCloser by doing nothing in Close.
    66	type readSeekerNopCloser struct {
    67	        io.ReadSeeker
    68	}
    69	
    70	// Close does nothing.
    71	func (r readSeekerNopCloser) Close() error {
    72	        return nil
    73	}

    75	// NewReadSeekerNoOpCloser creates a new ReadSeekerNoOpCloser with the given ReadSeeker.
    76	func NewReadSeekerNoOpCloser(r io.ReadSeeker) ReadSeekCloser {
    77	        return readSeekerNopCloser{r}
    78	}

    80	// NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString uses strings.NewReader to create a new ReadSeekerNoOpCloser
    81	// from the given string.
    82	func NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(content string) ReadSeekCloser {
    83	        return stringReadSeeker{s: content, readSeekerNopCloser: readSeekerNopCloser{strings.NewReader(content)}}
    84	}

   104	func NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromBytes(content []byte) readSeekerNopCloser {

   108	// NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromReader creates a new ReadSeekerNoOpCloser from the given io.Reader.
   109	// If the given io.Reader is not an io.ReadSeeker, the entire content will be read into memory.
   110	func NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromReader(r io.Reader) (readSeekerNopCloser, error) {
   111	        var rs io.ReadSeeker
   112	        if s, ok := r.(io.ReadSeeker); ok {
   113	                rs = s
   114	        } else {
   115	                b, err := io.ReadAll(r)
   116	                if err != nil {
   117	                        return readSeekerNopCloser{rs}, err
   118	                }
   119	                rs = bytes.NewReader(b)
   120	        }
   121	        return readSeekerNopCloser{rs}, nil
   122	}
   123	
   124	// NewOpenReadSeekCloser creates a new ReadSeekCloser from the given ReadSeeker.
   125	// The ReadSeeker will be seeked to the beginning before returned.
   126	func NewOpenReadSeekCloser(r ReadSeekCloser) OpenReadSeekCloser {
   127	        return func() (ReadSeekCloser, error) {
   128	                r.Seek(0, io.SeekStart)
   129	                return r, nil
   130	        }
   131	}
   132	
   133	// OpenReadSeekCloser allows setting some other way (than reading from a filesystem)
   134	// to open or create a ReadSeekCloser.

2026-05-29 21:47:22,866 - INFO - swea-agent-gohugoio__hugo-14685 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me look at how `ReadString` is used in `Content()`:

```go
func (l *genericResource) Content(context.Context) (any, error) {
    r, err := l.ReadSeekCloser()
    if err != nil {
        return "", err
    }
    defer r.Close()

    return hugio.ReadString(r)
}
```

And `ReadString` checks if the reader is a `StringReader` - if it is, it returns the original string directly (via `ReadString()`). The `stringReadSeeker` type is used for strings and it implements `StringReader` by returning the original string.

So far so good. Now let me trace the actual problem. Let me look at how `NewResource` from `ResourceSourceDescriptor` handles the `OpenReadSeekCloser`:

In `resource_spec.go`:
```go
func (r *Spec) NewResource(rd ResourceSourceDescriptor) (resource.Resource, error) {
    ...
    gr := &genericResource{
        ...
        sd: rd,
        ...
    }
    ...
}
```

The `sd` field is the `ResourceSourceDescriptor`. And `ReadSeekCloser()` just calls `l.sd.OpenReadSeekCloser()`.

Now let's look at the content_map_page_assembler.go again, specifically where resources from content adapters are handled:

```go
if rs.rc != nil && rs.rc.Content.IsResourceValue() {
    // Resource value path...
} else {
    ...
    rd := resources.ResourceSourceDescriptor{
        OpenReadSeekCloser:   rs.opener,
        ...
    }
    if rs.rc != nil {
        rc := rs.rc
        rd.OpenReadSeekCloser = rc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()
        ...
    }
    r, err := ps.s.ResourceSpec.NewResource(rd)
    ...
    rs.r = r
}
```

Wait, I notice something important here: `rs.opener` is set from `resourceSource`. Let me look at how `resourceSource` is created in `content_map.go` line 404:

```go
rs := &resourceSource{path: rc.PathInfo, rc: rc, opener: nil, fi: pt.GoTmplFi, sv: s.siteVector}
```

So `opener` is `nil`. Then in the assembler, `rd.OpenReadSeekCloser` is first set to `rs.opener` (nil), then overridden by `rc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()`.

But wait, let me look at `resourceSource` clone method:

```go
func (r resourceSource) clone() *resourceSource {
    r.state = resourceStateNew
    r.r = nil
    return &r
}
```

It sets `r.r = nil`. This is important because `r.r` is the cached resource. When the resource is cloned (e.g., for multiple sites/languages), the `r.r` is reset.

Now let me look at the issue from a different angle. The error "invalid JPEG format: short Huffman data" suggests that when reading the image data, the JPEG decoder reads incomplete data. This could happen if:

1. The string value is somehow corrupted
2. There's a race condition where the `OpenReadSeekCloser` is shared and one goroutine reads part of the data while another reads the rest
3. The `strings.NewReader` state (Seek position) is not properly reset

Let me look at the `NewOpenReadSeekCloser`:

```go
func NewOpenReadSeekCloser(r ReadSeekCloser) OpenReadSeekCloser {
    return func() (ReadSeekCloser, error) {
        r.Seek(0, io.SeekStart)
        return r, nil
    }
}
```

This creates a closure that returns the same `r` each time. But `r` is a `ReadSeekCloser` created from `NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(s.ValueAsString())`. 

Now look at `ValueAsString()`:

```go
func (s Source) ValueAsString() string {
    if s.Value == nil {
        return ""
    }
    ss, err := cast.ToStringE(s.Value)
    ...
}
```

And `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()`:

```go
func (s Source) ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser() hugio.OpenReadSeekCloser {
    return hugio.NewOpenReadSeekCloser(hugio.NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString(s.ValueAsString()))
}
```

Now here's the key insight: `ValueAsString()` is called ONCE when `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()` is called. But wait - it's called each time `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()` is called? No, actually `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()` is called once in the assembler:

```go
rd.OpenReadSeekCloser = rc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()
```

This creates a closure that captures the `ReadSeekCloser` created from the string. Each time the closure is called, it seeks back to 0 and returns the same reader.

But here's a potential issue: if `cast.ToStringE(s.Value)` is called on a `resource.Resource` (not a string), what happens? Let me check if `.Content` returns a string or something else.

Actually, let me reconsider. The PR says:

> creating a page resource (an image) by setting `content.value` to the string returned by a global resource's `.Content` value results in intermittent errors

So `content.value` is set to the string from `.Content`. But `.Content` returns `any`:

```go
func (l *genericResource) Content(context.Context) (any, error) {
    r, err := l.ReadSeekCloser()
    if err != nil {
        return "", err
    }
    defer r.Close()

    return hugio.ReadString(r)
}
```

`ReadString` first checks if it's a `StringReader`. For image resources, the `ReadSeekCloser` is probably from a file, not a string. So it would go to `io.ReadAll` and return the full content as a string. That string would then be passed to `content.value`.

Now, `ValueAsString()` is called on the `Source` struct. The `Value` field contains the string from `.Content`. `cast.ToStringE` should work fine for a string.

But wait - let me look at where `ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser` is called:

In `content_map_page_assembler.go` line 1233:
```go
rd.OpenReadSeekCloser = rc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser()
```

But also in `page__meta.go` line 352:
```go
openSource: pc.Content.ValueAsOpenReadSeekCloser(),
```

These are for different purposes: one for resources, one for pages. Both create a closure that returns the same `ReadSeekCloser`.

Now here's the potential race condition: the same `ReadSeekCloser` (strings.NewReader) is shared across multiple calls. `strings.NewReader` is not thread-safe. If two goroutines try to read from the same `strings.NewReader` simultaneously, they could interfere with each other.

But wait, the `ReadSeekCloser` is created from `NewReadSeekerNoOpCloserFromString` which wraps a `strings.NewReader`. The closure in `NewOpenReadSeekCloser` calls `r.Seek(0, io.SeekStart)` before returning. If one goroutine has already started reading and another seeks, the first goroutine would get corrupted data.

This is the race condition! The `OpenReadSeekCloser` closure returns the SAME `ReadSeekCloser` instance every time. If multiple goroutines try to read from it concurrently, they will interfere.

Let me verify this by looking at how resources are processed. Let me check if resources can be processed concurrently:
